   1: """Runs router — POST /runs, GET /runs/{id}, POST /runs/{id}/cancel.
   2: 
   3: I-phase0-005 (Codex APPROVE iter 4): persist runs to SQLite via
   4: polaris_v6.queue.run_store and enqueue the Dramatiq actor on POST.
   5: Replaces the previous in-memory `_run_table` dict.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-010 (#506): POST /runs resolves uploaded `document_ids` to content
   8: BEFORE inserting/enqueuing the run, so a missing or unparsed upload fails
   9: loud here rather than leaving a queued orphan run. The resolved content is
  10: embedded in the actor message because the Dramatiq worker is a separate
  11: process and cannot read the API process's in-memory upload table.
  12: 
  13: I-rdy-011 (#507): POST /runs/{id}/cancel — a queued run cancels instantly;
  14: an in-progress run records the cancel request (the worker observes it at
  15: the next pipeline stage boundary). Already-terminal runs are an idempotent
  16: no-op.
  17: 
  18: I-rdy-013 (#509): POST /runs enforces the 1-concurrent-session constraint
  19: via `run_store.insert_run_if_idle` — a 2nd concurrent request is cleanly
  20: rejected with HTTP 409 (never enqueued) and a structured detail the
  21: frontend renders as a link to the active run.
  22: """
  23: 
  24: from __future__ import annotations
  25: 
  26: import sqlite3
  27: import uuid
  28: 
  29: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  30: 
  31: from polaris_v6.api.upload import chunk_text, get_upload_record
  32: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  33: from polaris_v6.queue.actors import enqueue_research_run
  34: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_request import RunRequest
  35: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  36: 
  37: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["runs"])
  38: 
  39: 
  40: def _resolve_uploaded_documents(document_ids: list[str]) -> list[dict]:
  41:     """Resolve uploaded document_ids → content for actor-message embedding.
  42: 
  43:     Returns one dict per id: `{document_id, classification, filename,
  44:     chunks}`. `chunks` is `chunk_text(record.content)` — the full document
  45:     re-chunked (and capped), NOT the 3-chunk `chunk_preview`.
  46: 
  47:     Fails loud (HTTP 400) per LAW II on:
  48:       * a document_id with no upload record;
  49:       * an upload that yields no extractable text (e.g. an unparsed
  50:         pdf/docx) — a silent zero-evidence run would mislead the operator.
  51:     """
  52:     resolved: list[dict] = []
  53:     for document_id in document_ids:
  54:         record = get_upload_record(document_id)
  55:         if record is None:
  56:             raise HTTPException(
  57:                 status_code=400,
  58:                 detail=f"uploaded document {document_id!r} not found",
  59:             )
  60:         chunks = chunk_text(record.content)
  61:         if not chunks:
  62:             raise HTTPException(
  63:                 status_code=400,
  64:                 detail=(
  65:                     f"uploaded document {document_id!r} ({record.filename}) "
  66:                     "has no extractable text — pdf/docx parsing is not yet "
  67:                     "available; upload a .md or .txt document to ground a run."
  68:                 ),
  69:             )
  70:         resolved.append(
  71:             {
  72:                 "document_id": document_id,
  73:                 "classification": record.classification,
  74:                 "filename": record.filename,
  75:                 "chunks": chunks,
  76:             }
  77:         )
  78:     return resolved
  79: 
  80: 
  81: @router.post("", response_model=RunStatusResponse, status_code=202)
  82: def create_run(payload: RunRequest) -> RunStatusResponse:
  83:     # I-rdy-010: resolve uploads BEFORE insert_run/enqueue so a bad
  84:     # document_id fails loud here instead of orphaning a queued run.
  85:     uploaded_documents = _resolve_uploaded_documents(payload.document_ids)
  86: 
  87:     run_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
  88:     try:
  89:         # I-rdy-013: atomic 1-concurrent-session gate. Returns the blocking
  90:         # active run when rejected, None when this run was inserted.
  91:         active = run_store.insert_run_if_idle(
  92:             run_id, payload.template, payload.question
  93:         )
  94:     except sqlite3.IntegrityError as exc:
  95:         # uuid4 collision is theoretically impossible but defensive
  96:         raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail=f"run {run_id!r} already exists") from exc
  97:     except RuntimeError as exc:
  98:         # init_db permission-denied or similar
  99:         raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 100: 
 101:     if active is not None:
 102:         # I-rdy-013: 1-concurrent-session constraint — a research run is
 103:         # already queued or in progress. Reject cleanly; the rejected run is
 104:         # never enqueued (insert_run_if_idle rolled back — no row to clean
 105:         # up). The structured `detail` lets the frontend render a specific
 106:         # UX with a link to the active run.
 107:         raise HTTPException(
 108:             status_code=409,
 109:             detail={
 110:                 "code": "concurrent_run_active",
 111:                 "active_run_id": active.run_id,
 112:                 "active_status": active.lifecycle_status,
 113:                 "message": (
 114:                     "POLARIS runs one research session at a time. "
 115:                     f"Run {active.run_id[:8]} is currently {active.lifecycle_status}. "
 116:                     "Wait for it to finish before starting a new run."
 117:                 ),
 118:             },
 119:         )
 120: 
 121:     # The actor message carries the resolved upload content (the worker is
 122:     # a separate process — it cannot read the API process's upload table).
 123:     actor_payload = payload.model_dump()
 124:     actor_payload["uploaded_documents"] = uploaded_documents
 125:     try:
 126:         enqueue_research_run.send(run_id, actor_payload)
 127:     except Exception as exc:
 128:         # I-rdy-013 (Codex diff P1-001): the queued row is already committed.
 129:         # If enqueue fails it would never run yet would permanently hold the
 130:         # single-session slot. Mark it failed (terminal → frees the slot),
 131:         # then surface 503.
 132:         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"enqueue failed: {exc}")
 133:         raise HTTPException(
 134:             status_code=503,
 135:             detail=f"failed to enqueue run {run_id!r}: {exc}",
 136:         ) from exc
 137: 
 138:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 139:     if record is None:  # pragma: no cover — insert just succeeded
 140:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after insert")
 141:     return record
 142:

 144: @router.get("", response_model=list[RunStatusResponse])
 145: def list_runs(status: str = "completed", limit: int = 20) -> list[RunStatusResponse]:
 146:     """List completed runs newest-first (I-cd-705 / #705).
 147: 
 148:     Feeds the compare picker (#543), follow-up picker (#542), and the home
 149:     recent-runs strip. Only `status=completed` is supported today; aborted
 150:     runs are excluded by run_store.list_completed_runs (not
 151:     EvidenceContract-usable). `limit` is clamped to [1, 100].
 152:     """
 153:     if status != "completed":
 154:         raise HTTPException(
 155:             status_code=400,
 156:             detail="only status=completed is supported",
 157:         )
 158:     limit = max(1, min(limit, 100))
 159:     return run_store.list_completed_runs(limit=limit)

 162: @router.get("/{run_id}", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 163: def get_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 164:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 165:     if record is None:
 166:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 167:     return record

 170: @router.post("/{run_id}/cancel", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 171: def cancel_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 172:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011 / #507).
 173: 
 174:     - Unknown run → 404.
 175:     - Already terminal (completed / failed / cancelled) → idempotent no-op,
 176:       returns the current record (200).
 177:     - queued → cancelled instantly; in_progress → cancel requested, the
 178:       worker aborts cooperatively at the next pipeline stage boundary.
 179:     """
 180:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 181:     if record is None:
 182:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 183:     if record.lifecycle_status in run_store.TERMINAL_STATUSES:
 184:         return record  # idempotent — nothing to cancel
 185: 
 186:     run_store.request_cancel(run_id)
 187: 
 188:     updated = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 189:     if updated is None:  # pragma: no cover — the row existed a line ago
 190:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after cancel")
 191:     return updated

   1: "use client";
   2: 
   3: import Link from "next/link";
   4: import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
   5: 
   6: import { authHeader } from "@/lib/auth";
   7: 
   8: // I-cd-ui-001 (#704): home recent-runs strip. Consumes the GET /api/v6/runs
   9: // list endpoint (#705). The home is PUBLIC and the runs endpoint is
  10: // auth-gated (bearer token), so this MUST degrade to null on 401 / any
  11: // failure / empty — never an error and never a /sign-in redirect (that is
  12: // why it uses authHeader() directly, not authFetch which redirects).
  13: 
  14: type RunRow = {
  15:   run_id: string;
  16:   template: string;
  17:   question: string;
  18:   finished_at: string | null;
  19: };
  20: 
  21: function formatFinished(value: string | null): string | null {
  22:   if (!value) return null;
  23:   const d = new Date(value);
  24:   if (Number.isNaN(d.getTime())) return null; // tolerate malformed finished_at
  25:   return d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, {
  26:     month: "short",
  27:     day: "numeric",
  28:   });
  29: }
  30: 
  31: export function RecentRunsStrip() {
  32:   const [runs, setRuns] = useState<RunRow[]>([]);
  33: 
  34:   useEffect(() => {
  35:     let cancelled = false;
  36:     (async () => {
  37:       try {
  38:         const res = await fetch("/api/v6/runs?status=completed&limit=5", {
  39:           headers: authHeader(),
  40:         });
  41:         if (!res.ok) return; // 401 (logged-out) or any non-ok → render nothing
  42:         const data: unknown = await res.json();
  43:         if (!cancelled && Array.isArray(data)) {
  44:           setRuns(data as RunRow[]);
  45:         }
  46:       } catch {
  47:         // network / parse failure → render nothing
  48:       }
  49:     })();
  50:     return () => {
  51:       cancelled = true;
  52:     };
  53:   }, []);
  54: 
  55:   if (runs.length === 0) return null;
  56: 
  57:   return (
  58:     <section
  59:       aria-labelledby="recent_runs_heading"
  60:       className="flex flex-col gap-3"
  61:     >
  62:       <h2
  63:         id="recent_runs_heading"
  64:         className="text-muted-foreground text-xs font-medium tracking-widest uppercase"
  65:       >
  66:         Recent verifications
  67:       </h2>
  68:       <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2" data-testid="recent-runs-strip">
  69:         {runs.map((run) => {
  70:           const finished = formatFinished(run.finished_at);
  71:           return (
  72:             <Link
  73:               key={run.run_id}
  74:               href={`/runs/${run.run_id}`}
  75:               data-testid={`recent-run-${run.run_id}`}
  76:               className="border-border bg-card hover:border-primary/40 focus-visible:ring-ring group flex max-w-xs flex-col gap-1 rounded-lg border px-3 py-2 transition-colors focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:outline-none"
  77:             >
  78:               <span className="text-primary text-[10px] font-semibold tracking-widest uppercase">
  79:                 {run.template}
  80:                 {finished ? (
  81:                   <span className="text-muted-foreground font-normal">
  82:                     {" · "}
  83:                     {finished}
  84:                   </span>
  85:                 ) : null}
  86:               </span>
  87:               <span className="text-foreground line-clamp-2 text-sm">
  88:                 {run.question}
  89:               </span>
  90:             </Link>
  91:           );
  92:         })}
  93:       </div>
  94:     </section>
  95:   );
  96: }

 532:     I-cd-017 (#627): pin-replay timeseries source. Uses the existing
 533:     `idx_runs_query_slug` index. Returns `[]` (not None) when no rows
 534:     match — callers distinguish "anchor run exists but no completed
 535:     siblings" from "anchor run unknown" via get_run() before calling.
 536: 
 537:     Defensive against missing-table / legacy-schema like get_run.
 538:     """
 539:     query = (
 540:         f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 541:         "WHERE query_slug=? AND lifecycle_status='completed' "
 542:         "ORDER BY finished_at ASC"
 543:     )
 544:     conn = _connect(path)
 545:     try:
 546:         try:
 547:             rows = conn.execute(query, (query_slug,)).fetchall()
 548:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 549:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 550:             if "no such table" in msg:
 551:                 return []
 552:             if "no such column" in msg:
 553:                 conn.close()
 554:                 init_db(path)
 555:                 conn = _connect(path)
 556:                 rows = conn.execute(query, (query_slug,)).fetchall()
 557:             else:
 558:                 raise
 559:     finally:
 560:         conn.close()
 561:     return [_row_to_response(row) for row in rows]
 562: 
 563: 
 564: def list_completed_runs(
 565:     limit: int = 20, *, path: str | None = None
 566: ) -> list[RunStatusResponse]:
 567:     """List completed, non-aborted runs newest-first (finished_at DESC), capped.
 568: 
 569:     I-cd-705 (#705): source for GET /api/v6/runs — the compare picker (#543),
 570:     follow-up picker (#542), and home recent-runs strip. Excludes
 571:     `abort_*` pipeline_status (not EvidenceContract-usable). release_allowed
 572:     is a per-run manifest flag (too heavy to read in a list query) and is
 573:     enforced DOWNSTREAM at bundle/followup/compare fetch time (#680), so a
 574:     release-blocked partial may appear here but 422s when actually opened.
 575: 
 576:     Defensive against missing-table / legacy-schema like get_run.
 577: 
 578:     Codex iter-1 P2: clamp limit to [1, 100] HERE too, so direct in-process
 579:     callers are safe even though the HTTP route also clamps.
 580:     """
 581:     limit = max(1, min(limit, 100))
 582:     query = (
 583:         f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 584:         "WHERE lifecycle_status='completed' "
 585:         "AND (pipeline_status IS NULL OR pipeline_status NOT LIKE 'abort\\_%' ESCAPE '\\') "
 586:         "ORDER BY finished_at DESC LIMIT ?"
 587:     )
 588:     conn = _connect(path)
 589:     try:
 590:         try:
 591:             rows = conn.execute(query, (limit,)).fetchall()
 592:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 593:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 594:             if "no such table" in msg:
 595:                 return []
 596:             if "no such column" in msg:
 597:                 conn.close()
 598:                 init_db(path)
 599:                 conn = _connect(path)
 600:                 rows = conn.execute(query, (limit,)).fetchall()
 601:             else:
 602:                 raise
 603:     finally:
 604:         conn.close()
 605:     return [_row_to_response(row) for row in rows]

import { writeFileSync } from "node:fs";
import path from "node:path";
import { expect, test, type Page } from "@playwright/test";

type Row = { d: string; e: string; v: "PASS" | "FAIL"; obs: string };
const transcript: Row[] = [];
const TRANSCRIPT_PATH = path.resolve(
  __dirname,
  "../../../outputs/audits/I-f2-008/walkthrough_transcript.md",
);

const baseDecision = {
  status: "in_scope",
  scope_class: "clinical_efficacy",
  ambiguity_axes: [],
  clarifications_needed: [],
  provenance: {},
  decision_id: "wt",
  decided_at_utc: new Date().toISOString(),
  latency_ms: 1,
};

async function intakeMock(page: Page, dec: object) {
  await page.route("**/api/intake", async (r) =>
    r.fulfill({
      status: 200,
      contentType: "application/json",
      body: JSON.stringify({
        error: false,
        decision: { ...baseDecision, ...dec },
        server_time_utc: new Date().toISOString(),
      }),
    }),
  );
}

async function disambigMock(page: Page, n: number, isAmb = true) {
  await page.route("**/api/disambiguation", async (r) =>
    r.fulfill({
      status: 200,
      contentType: "application/json",
      body: JSON.stringify({
        is_ambiguous: isAmb,
        num_clusters: n,
        clusters: Array.from({ length: n }, (_, i) => ({
          cluster_id: i,
          label: `label_${i}`,
          sample_snippets: [`s${i}`],
        })),
        server_time_utc: new Date().toISOString(),
      }),
    }),
  );
}

async function record(d: string, e: string, fn: () => Promise<void>) {
  try {
    await fn();
    transcript.push({ d, e, v: "PASS", obs: "ok" });
  } catch (err) {
    transcript.push({
      d,
      e,
      v: "FAIL",
      obs: err instanceof Error ? err.message.slice(0, 60) : String(err),
    });
    throw err;
  }
}

test.skip(
  ({ browserName }) => browserName !== "chromium",
  "f2 walkthrough is chromium-only",
);

test("F2 walkthrough — 22 scenarios", async ({ page }) => {
  const candidates = (n: number) =>
    Array.from({ length: n }, (_, i) => ({ text: `s${i}`, embedding: [i, 0] }));
  const submit = async (q: string) => {
    await page.goto("/intake");
    await page.getByTestId("intake-question-input").fill(q);
    await page.getByTestId("intake-submit").click();
  };

  for (const { q, n } of [
    { q: "BPEI", n: 3 },
    { q: "MS treatment options", n: 2 },
    { q: "PR campaign metrics", n: 5 },
  ]) {
    await intakeMock(page, {
      needs_disambiguation: true,
      candidate_snippets: candidates(n),
    });
    await disambigMock(page, n);
    await record(`amb:${q}`, `${n} cards`, async () => {
      await submit(q);
      await expect(
        page.locator('[data-testid^="disambiguation-cluster-"]'),
      ).toHaveCount(n);
    });
    await page.unrouteAll();
  }

  for (const q of [
    "Does tirzepatide reduce A1c in adults with type 2 diabetes?",
    "What are the safety risks of metformin in older adults?",
    "Is aspirin effective for headaches in adults?",
  ]) {
    await intakeMock(page, { needs_disambiguation: false });
    let calls = 0;
    await page.route("**/api/disambiguation", (r) => {
      calls++;
      r.abort();
    });
    await record(`unamb:${q.slice(0, 24)}`, "no modal", async () => {
      await submit(q);
      await expect(page.getByTestId("scope-decision-view")).toBeVisible();
      await page.waitForTimeout(120);
      await expect(
        page.locator('[data-slot="disambiguation-modal"]'),
      ).toBeHidden();
      expect(calls).toBe(0);
    });
    await page.unrouteAll();
  }

  for (const i of [0, 1, 2]) {
    await intakeMock(page, {
      needs_disambiguation: true,
      candidate_snippets: candidates(2),
    });
    await disambigMock(page, 2, false);
    await record(`guard:${i}`, "modal hidden", async () => {
      await submit("Does X reduce Y?");
      await expect(page.getByTestId("scope-decision-view")).toBeVisible();
      await page.waitForTimeout(120);
      await expect(
        page.locator('[data-slot="disambiguation-modal"]'),
      ).toBeHidden();
    });
    await page.unrouteAll();
  }

  for (const fr of [
    "Quels sont les effets secondaires de la metformine?",
    "Est-ce que l'aspirine est efficace pour les maux de tête?",
    "La thérapie physique aide-t-elle pour les douleurs lombaires?",
  ]) {
    let intakeCalls = 0;
    await page.route("**/api/intake", (r) => {
      intakeCalls++;
      r.fulfill({ status: 500, body: "x" });
    });
    await record(`fr:${fr.slice(0, 24)}`, "English error", async () => {
      await submit(fr);
      await expect(page.getByTestId("intake-error")).toContainText("English");
      expect(intakeCalls).toBe(0);
    });
    await page.unrouteAll();
  }

  for (const { name, type, banner } of [
    { name: "test.pdf", type: "application/pdf", banner: true },
    { name: "test.PDF", type: "", banner: true },
    { name: "test.txt", type: "text/plain", banner: false },
  ]) {
    await record(`pdf:${name}`, banner ? "banner" : "no banner", async () => {
      await page.goto("/intake");
      await expect(page.getByTestId("pdf-drop-ready")).toHaveAttribute(
        "data-ready",
        "1",
      );
      await page.evaluate(
        ({ name, type }) => {
          const dt = new DataTransfer();
          dt.items.add(new File([], name, { type }));
          window.dispatchEvent(
            new DragEvent("drop", {
              dataTransfer: dt,
              bubbles: true,
              cancelable: true,
            }),
          );
        },
        { name, type },
      );
      if (banner) {
        await expect(page.getByTestId("pdf-drop-banner")).toBeVisible();
      } else {
        await page.waitForTimeout(120);
        await expect(page.getByTestId("pdf-drop-banner")).toBeHidden();
      }
    });
  }

  await record("edge:empty", "3-char gate", async () => {
    await page.goto("/intake");
    await page.getByTestId("intake-submit").click();
    await expect(page.getByTestId("intake-error")).toContainText(
      "3 characters",
    );
  });
  await record("edge:whitespace", "3-char gate", async () => {
    await page.goto("/intake");
    await page.getByTestId("intake-question-input").fill("   ");
    await page.getByTestId("intake-submit").click();
    await expect(page.getByTestId("intake-error")).toContainText(
      "3 characters",
    );
  });
  let intakeCalls2 = 0;
  await page.route("**/api/intake", (r) => {
    intakeCalls2++;
    r.abort();
  });
  await record("edge:long", "input capped 2000", async () => {
    await page.goto("/intake");
    await page.getByTestId("intake-question-input").fill("a".repeat(2500));
    expect(
      (await page.getByTestId("intake-question-input").inputValue()).length,
    ).toBe(2000);
    expect(intakeCalls2).toBe(0);
  });
  await page.unrouteAll();

  for (const cid of [0, 1, 2]) {
    await intakeMock(page, {
      needs_disambiguation: true,
      candidate_snippets: candidates(3),
    });
    await disambigMock(page, 3);
    await record(`pick:${cid}`, `label_${cid}`, async () => {
      await submit("BPEI");
      await expect(
        page.getByTestId(`disambiguation-cluster-${cid}`),
      ).toBeVisible();
      await page.getByTestId(`disambiguation-cluster-${cid}`).click();
      await expect(page.getByTestId("disambig-picked-label")).toHaveText(
        `label_${cid}`,
      );
    });
    await page.unrouteAll();
  }

  await intakeMock(page, {
    needs_disambiguation: true,
    candidate_snippets: candidates(3),
  });
  await disambigMock(page, 3);
  await record("cancel", "no write", async () => {
    await submit("BPEI");
    await expect(page.getByTestId("disambiguation-cluster-0")).toBeVisible();
    await page.keyboard.press("Escape");
    await expect(page.getByTestId("disambig-picked-label")).toHaveText("");
  });

  expect(transcript.length).toBe(22);
  expect(transcript.every((r) => r.v === "PASS")).toBe(true);
});

test.afterAll(async ({}, testInfo) => {
  if (testInfo.project.name !== "chromium") return;
  const passed = transcript.filter((r) => r.v === "PASS").length;
  const lines = [
    "# F2 Walkthrough Transcript (auto-generated)",
    "",
    `Run: ${new Date().toISOString()} / ${passed}/${transcript.length} PASS`,
    "",
    "| # | Description | Expected | Verdict | Observed |",
    "|---|---|---|---|---|",
    ...transcript.map(
      (r, i) => `| ${i + 1} | ${r.d} | ${r.e} | ${r.v} | ${r.obs} |`,
    ),
  ];
  writeFileSync(TRANSCRIPT_PATH, lines.join("\n") + "\n", "utf8");
});
